- There is a hidden, unchanging, target number. Your group must make your individual numbers sum exactly to that target.

- Players do NOT see other players' individual submissions — only the group total.
- The game ends when the group sum equals the target, or after the maximum number of rounds. The current round number and rounds remaining are shown each turn.
